***fossiel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fossiel.html>fossiel</a> (18632)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">fossile</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fossilis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">something which <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> dug up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fodio</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I dig up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First attested in the early 19th century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fossiel.html>fossiel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fossielen.html>fossielen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">fossiliën</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fossiel.html>fossieltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">fossil</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> someone with very old fashioned ideas, a dinosaur</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fouilleren.html>fouilleren</a> (10923)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">fouiller</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fouilleren.html>fouilleren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to search, to frisk</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***fout.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fout.html>fout</a> (554)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">faute</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">faute</i>. The adjectival sense developed <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a>, replacing older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:foutief.html>foutief</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fout.html>fout</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fouten.html>fouten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:foutje.html>foutje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>error</li>
<li>mistake</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fout.html>fout</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fouter.html>fouter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">foutst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>wrong</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> unfashionable, cheesy, inappropriate</li>

***fractuur.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fractuur.html>fractuur</a> (65135)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">fracture</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">fracture</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fractura</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a breach, fracture, cleft</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">frangere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to break</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, past participle <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fractus</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰreg-</i>, from whence also English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">break</i> and Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:breken.html>breken</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>franc</a> (11961)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>franc</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/franc" class="extiw" title="w:franc"><a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>franc</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/franc" class="extiw" title="w:franc">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>franc</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:francs.html>francs</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A former unit of currency of France, Belgium and Luxembourg, replaced by the euro.</li>
<li>Any of several units of currency, some of which are multi-national (West African CFA <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>Franc</a> (XOF), Central African CFA <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>Franc</a> (XAF), the Swiss <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>franc</a> (CHF)) while others are national currencies.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The word <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>franc</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> abbreviated 'F' in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_4217" class="extiw" title="w:ISO 4217">ISO 4217</a> currency <a href = vnd.unilang:codes.html>codes</a>, usually prepended by the country's 2-letter alpha code in the case of national currencies:
</p>
<ul><li>BIF: Burundi <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>Franc</a></li>
<li>CDF: Congolese <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>Franc</a></li>
<li>CHF: Swiss <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>franc</a></li>
<li>DJF: Djibouti <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>Franc</a></li>
<li>GNF: Guinean <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>Franc</a></li>
<li>KMF: Comorian <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>Franc</a></li>
<li>RAF: Rwandan <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>Franc</a></li>
<li>XAF: Central African <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>Franc</a></li>
<li>XOF: West African <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>Franc</a></li></ul>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:franciscaan.html>franciscaan</a> (61044)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Franciscānus</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">Franciscus</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-aan</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:franciscaan.html>franciscaan</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:franciscanen.html>franciscanen</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">franciscanes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A Franciscan, typically a male Franciscan monk.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">fremineur</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">minderbroeder</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li>kloosterling <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:bedel.html>bedel</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:orde.html>orde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heilige.html>heilige</a> Franciscus <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:assisi.html>Assisi</a></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:franciscaner.html>franciscaner</a> (106717)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:franciscaan.html>franciscaan</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:franciscaner.html>franciscaner</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Franciscan
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">franciscaans</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Chiefly used of people, organisations and buildings, having a narrower range than <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">franciscaans</i>.
</p>

</p>

***frater.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:frater.html>frater</a> (54502)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:frater.html>frater</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:frater.html>frater</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Italic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Italic language">Proto-Italic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="itc-pro">*frātēr</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰréh₂tēr</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Catholicism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a candidate for priesthood</li></ol>

***frauderen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:frauderen.html>frauderen</a> (33405)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:frauderen.html>frauderen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">frauder</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:frauderen.html>frauderen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to commit fraud</li></ol>
